## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models population growth rate dP/dt as a function of population size P and time t, which is the core problem of population dynamics. The inclusion of time as an explicit variable suggests possible non-autonomous effects like seasonal forcing, time-varying carrying capacity, or time-dependent harvesting.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (unlimited growth, Malthusian model)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (asymmetric sigmoidal growth)
- Theta-logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Allee effect (strong): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P) (minimum viable population threshold)
- Logistic with harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (constant yield harvesting)
- Proportional harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P (effort-based harvesting)
- Seasonally forced logistic: dP_dt = c0 * (1 + c1 * sin(c2 * t)) * P * (1 - c3 * P) (periodic environmental variation)
- Time-varying growth rate: dP_dt = c0 * exp(c1 * t) * P (exponentially changing growth rate)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (contest competition)
- Logistic with immigration: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) + c2 (constant immigration rate)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) * c3 (flexible growth curve)
- Polynomial density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (higher-order density effects)
- Time-decaying capacity: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P * exp(c2 * t)) (degrading environment)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope â†’ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects â†’ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay â†’ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior â†’ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects â†’ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent regulation â†’ multiplicative factor (1 - c*P) or rational form 1/(1 + c*P) attached to growth term
- Allee effect (positive density dependence at low P) â†’ additional multiplicative factor (P - c) creating a minimum population threshold
- Immigration/emigration â†’ additive constant term independent of P in the growth rate equation
- Seasonal or periodic environmental forcing â†’ growth rate parameters modulated by sin(c*t) or cos(c*t)
- Carrying capacity structure â†’ dP/dt = 0 at a specific nonzero P value, implying P appears in a factor that creates a root
- Contest vs. scramble competition â†’ Beverton-Holt form P/(1+c*P) for contest, P*(1-c*P) for scramble
- Environmental degradation over time â†’ carrying capacity or growth rate multiplied by monotonically decreasing function of t
- Cubic or higher-order P terms â†’ bistability or multiple equilibria in population dynamics
- Depensation in fisheries â†’ growth rate per capita (dP_dt/P) that is non-monotonic in P
- Delayed maturation or stage structure approximation â†’ growth rate depending on both P and a time-lag proxy like t
